The technical know-how and experience acquired within the scope of consulting services have supported our departments that are working on other projects while the corporate experience fed by the operations in such fields has contributed considerably to our consultancy services.","numberOfEmployees":{"value":1430,"@type":"QuantitativeValue"},"logo":{"contentUrl":"https://media.licdn.com/dms/image/v2/D4D0BAQEIs0Ty3WTTCg/company-logo_200_200/B4DZiiMkyYHsAI-/0/1755067862735/stmdefence_logo?e=2147483647&v=beta&t=P5Kz-aSa4GmW9PTdrOVjllwmT2evPI7Q-HEP1wgTLFg","description":"STM","@type":"ImageObject"},"slogan":"Engineering The Next | Sınırsız Teknolojiler, Güvenli Yarınlar #MilliMühendislik","sameAs":"http://www.stm.com.tr"}]}

    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              STM Savunma Teknolojileri Mühendislik ve Ticaret A.Ş. also known as STM, was established in 1991 to render project management, engineering, and consultancy services to the Presidency of Defence Industries (SSB) and the Turkish Armed Forces (TSK) in areas where high technology is involved. Since then, STM has carried out such duties successfully while introducing various critical technologies to our country. STM has also been a leader in bringing domestic contribution rate in the Turkish Defence Industry up to its current level by bringing on board qualified expert personnel that is much needed for the procurement of high technology defence systems and the transfer of such technologies.


STM has combined its work in various defence industry projects focusing on different software and platforms with its engineering know-how and the experience it has acquired over the years; this has led to the development of various projects and products in addition to its consulting activities. The technical know-how and experience acquired within the scope of consulting services have supported our departments that are working on other projects while the corporate experience fed by the operations in such fields has contributed considerably to our consultancy services.
          </p>

          <dl class="mt-6">
              
    <div class="mb-2 flex papabear:mr-3 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:flex-wrap" data-test-id="about-us__website">
      <dt class="font-sans text-md font-bold text-color-text break-words w-40 papabear:flex-shrink-0 papabear:mr-3 mamabear:flex-shrink-0 mamabear:mr-3 babybear:mb-1">
          Web Sitesi
      </dt>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We showcased our underwater technologies at <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fseabedsecurity2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SeabedSecurity2025</a> 🌊

As STM, we presented our submarine engineering and unmanned underwater systems, sharing our vision for maritime security with international delegations.⚓

📆 Sept 30 – Oct 1  
📍Troia | Portugal 🇵🇹
------
<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fseabedsecurity2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#SeabedSecurity2025</a>’te sualtı teknolojilerimizi sergiledik. 🌊

STM olarak, denizaltı mühendisliği ve insansız sualtı sistemlerimizi tanıtarak, deniz güvenliğine yönelik vizyonumuzu uluslararası delegasyonlarla paylaştık.⚓

📆 30 Eylül - 1 Ekim
 📍Troia | Portekiz 🇵🇹</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">🚢 TCG KINALIADA (F-514), 6 yıl önce bugün Türk Donanması’na teslim edilerek, %70'in üzerindeki yerlilik oranıyla milli gemi mühendisliğimizin gurur kaynağı oldu. ⚓

Dizayndan sistem tedarikine, entegrasyondan ana tahrik teminine kadar her aşamasında kritik görevler aldığımız TCG KINALIADA Korvetimiz ve kahraman personeline, göreve başlangıçlarının yıl dönümünde, emniyetli seyirler diliyoruz.🌊

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Preveze Deniz Zaferi’nin 487. yıl dönümü ve Deniz Kuvvetleri Günü kutlu olsun! 🇹🇷⚓

Zaferin yıl dönümünde Kaptan-ı Derya Barbaros Hayrettin Paşa’yı, şanlı ecdadımızı, tüm şehit ve gazilerimizi rahmet, minnet ve saygıyla anıyoruz.</p>
